     /* <![CDATA[ */
                     jQuery(document).ready(function(){
     ( function($) {   
         jQuery.ajax({
             url: "/search",
             type: 'GET',
             success: function(data) {
                 $('div#shopping-cart').html($(data).find('div.header-inner-right-wrapper.clearfix.pull-right').html());
             },
         });
     } ) ( jQuery );
 });
 
 jQuery(document).ready(function($){
     $(document).ready(function(){    
         $(".dropdown-cart").mouseover(function(){
             $(".dropdown-cart").css("background-color", "yellow");
         });
     });
 });
 
 jQuery(document).ready(function($){
     $('div.relatedthumb:eq(0)').css("margin-left","0px");
 });
 
 jQuery(document).ready(function($){
     $('table').css("width","").addClass("table");
     $('table').css("height","");
 });
 
 jQuery( document ).ready(function($){
 
     
     $( "#search-dealer-locator" ).on( "click", function() {
 
         var form = document.getElementById("dealer-form");
         var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
         var address = document.getElementById("LW3ZIP").value;
 
         geocoder.geocode( { 'address': address}, function(results, status) {
 
         if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
             var latitude = results[0].geometry.location.lat();
             var longitude = results[0].geometry.location.lng(); 
 
             $('#LW3LAT').attr('value', latitude);
             $('#LW3LON').attr('value', longitude);
             form.submit();
                    
             } 
 
         });   
     });
 
 
 });                /* ]]> */
    </script>
